This is a ranking of the best movesets in Pokémon GO for every Pokémon after they can have 2 charge moves. The calculation counts in coverage against all types. Due to that you wont see many pokemon where both charge moves have the same type (which also would not make sense in the game, because one move would always outclass the other one).
